    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText630298679197387536" style="display:none">For twenty-one-year-old Sydney, being in love with Kyler isn't anything new. They'd been best friends ever since he pushed her down on the playground and she made him eat a mud pie. Somewhere over the years, she fell for him and fell hard. The big problem with that? Kyler puts the 'man' in man-whore. He's never stayed with a girl longer than a few nights, and with it being their last year in college, Syd doesn't want to risk their friendship by declaring her love. <br /><br />Kyler has always put Syd on a pedestal that was too high for him to reach. To him, she's perfect and she's everything. But the feelings he has for her, he's always hidden away or focused on any other female. After all, Kyler will always be the poor boy from the wrong side of tracks, and Syd will always be the one girl he can never have. <br /><br />But when they're stranded together at a posh ski resort due to a massive Nor'easter, there's nothing stopping their red-hot feelings for each other from coming to the surface. Can their friendship survive the attraction? Better yet, can they survive at all? Because as the snow falls, someone is stalking them, and this ski trip may be a life-changer in more ways than one.</span>

house at the ski-resort during a snow storm, which forces them to spend time with each other, and to admit to their feelings.<br><br><br>I've kept the story thing short cause honestly, you don't need it's getting more difficult seeing him over and over again with his string of one night stands.<br>When she's forced to spend time alone with him, she can't deny how she feels anymore...<br><br>How I liked her...<br>Difficult to describe because on one hand, I felt really bad for her every time there was a misunderstanding between them, one scene made me cry :((( <br>But on the other hand, it could all be avoided if she only used a bit of her brain instead of jumping to conclusions :(((<br><br><br><br><br><b>Kyler</b><br><br><img always thinking he's not good enough for her :(((<br>But then, for him, no one is good enough for Sidney :D<br>When they get trapped during the storm, he'll find that he can't fight his attraction...<br><br>How I loved him...<br>Easy to describe cause I loved him a lot &lt;3<br>Gosh, he is just amazing and I love every chapter from his POV &lt;3 <br>He is uber-swoony, the things he says &lt;3 OMG! But then as a guy, he's a bit thick in the head and does the wrong thing sometimes :(( <br>But I don't care, I still loved him :)))<br><br><br><br><br><b>The sex</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419475ra/831643.gif" alt="Image &lt;br /&gt;Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It has to be mentioned cause this is NA and not every book is the same regarding the sexy times, but this one... very very hot :)<br>They are both 21, in case you're wondering so it isn't icky to read bwahhahha<br>The "education" scene, oh my. Very nice :D <br>And even though the one against the window was all wrong, it was still uber hot.<br>So for those of you who like a bit hotter NA, this will be PERFECT :)<br><br><br><br><br><b>Overall<br><br>The writing</b> - LOVED the dual POV, and I mean LOVED! It was <br>amazing to see both sides, especially his *sigh*, and especially in the sex scenes bwahahahahhah<br><br><b>The characters</b> - There are two other characters introduced that I'm betting will have a book of their own in this series. Me likey.<br>Something about Kyler and Sydney... the thing that bothered me most here and why it's a 4 star rating is the constant misunderstandings and jumping to conclusions :(<br>I don't like that in any scenario, well Ok a few times but through all the book?<br>I don't think they had a convo that didn't somehow end up totally misinterpreted. Oh well.<br>Other than that they were both pretty great, especially Kyler &lt;3 <br><br><b>The romance</b> - uber swoony and sometimes just sweet, but not yucky sweet that makes you want to throw up :) The one where you go all mushy and gooey (like the heroine here did often ahahahhaha)<br><br><b>The angst</b> - For those of you who are used to uber-angst, you probably won't find it here, but me? I don't read angsty and this WAS angsty to me, so I am happy with myself and the fact that I handled it and I didn't mind it at all :))))<br><br>The first half of the book was amazing, simply brilliant, 10 star material, but near the end something happened that just lowered my enthusiasm I guess, nothing bad but I wished it stayed the pace it had from the beginning :))<br><br><br><b>In the end, I recommend this book to everyone because it really was so lovely, wonderfully romantic, too damn hot, and just an easy read &lt;3<br><br>PS: This book does not have a cliffy or anything of the sort,the ending is wonderful &lt;3</b><br><br>*buddy read with V &lt;3*</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer656429864" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9718202447030669833"><b>VERY LOW 4 stars!!! BUT I still loved SOOO much about this book! </b><br/><br/>Frigid is NOT my favorite book by this very talented authors, and as much as I loved it, I did have a few issues. The constant misunderstandings and lack of communication throughout this <b>WHOLE</b> friends-to-lovers trope became tedious and tiring after awhile. And even though I liked both of the main characters, Kyler's voracious man-whoring ways was more of a turn <b>OFF</b> for me, <b>NOT</b> a turn on. I still fell in love with him but he was no </span>
  <span id="freeText9718202447030669833" style="display:none"><b>VERY LOW 4 stars!!! BUT I still loved SOOO much about this book! </b><br /><br />Frigid is NOT my favorite book by this very talented authors, and as much as I loved it, I did have a few issues. The constant misunderstandings and lack of communication throughout this <b>WHOLE</b> friends-to-lovers trope became tedious and tiring after awhile. And even though I liked both of the main characters, Kyler's voracious man-whoring ways was more of a turn <b>OFF</b> for me, <b>NOT</b> a turn on. I still fell in love with him but he was no <b>Cam</b>, <b>Daemon</b>, or <b>Hunter</b>! As for Sydney, my heart ached for her throughout most of this story. I found her character endearing and sweet but her constant lamenting and pining over her feelings for Kyler bordered on the pathetic and made her out to be somewhat of a doormat and a pessimists where he was concerned. <br /><br /><b>All that said, I very much enjoyed reading this story. I was captivated, enthralled, and drawn in by this couple's complex and endearing friendship. These two very <i>human</i> and charming characters have been in love with each other for years, and I couldn't get enough of their witty dialogue, complicated feeling, and off-the-charts chemistry. They brought this story to life for me and I stayed up most of the night reading their imperfectly perfect LOVE story. Other than a few hiccups, everything about this book is what I love in a good romance.</b><br /><br />Frigid is a charming, fun, well written, and steamy friends-to-lovers story. The happy for now ending was AMAZING! It left me feeling giddy, dreamy, and with a HUGE smile on my face. <br /><br /><b>J Lynn/Jennifer L Armentrout is one of my FAVORITE authors and I highly recommend this book.</b><br /><br />Enjoy! <br /><br />Note: For those wondering who the characters of Cam, Daemon, and Hunter are and what books they are from, here is the answer:<br /><br />Cam is the hero from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a><br />Daemon is the hero from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a> (The Lux series)<br />Hunter is the hero from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14060046.Obsession" title="Obsession by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsession</a> (Standalone book but part of the Lux series) </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669067534" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5469175538050454669">I can't believe this book. It was so, what's the word? Awful? <br/><br/>I know it's Jennifer Armentrout we're talking about but sadly all of her books (except Covenant Series) have the same bland characters. I remember lusting over Daemon when Obsidian first came out but now I just can't remember why. Most people, who obsessively read new adult novels will love her every book but I just wish it had more substance. Something other than a girl with self-esteem issues, a guy who has abs to die for and a mile</span>
  <span id="freeText5469175538050454669" style="display:none">I can't believe this book. It was so, what's the word? Awful? <br /><br />I know it's Jennifer Armentrout we're talking about but sadly all of her books (except Covenant Series) have the same bland characters. I remember lusting over Daemon when Obsidian first came out but now I just can't remember why. Most people, who obsessively read new adult novels will love her every book but I just wish it had more substance. Something other than a girl with self-esteem issues, a guy who has abs to die for and a mile long peen. It's getting pretty old and the sex scenes weren't that interesting because I felt like I read them in another NA novel. Why doesn't anyone write a book about a nerdy guy and a freaky girl getting stuck together on a project or something? I don't know, something like that. Why do they always have to be hot, supermodels?<br /><br />Sorry for rambling. The reason I didn't like Frigid, aside from the obvious one- repetitive type of characters, it was hard for me to <i>see</i> these two pining over each other for years. Sure, they mention how they hated seeing the other person with someone else but I didn't felt it. And then you have the <i>forever</i> speech in the end. How can they think they will be unbreakable after they only spend a couple of days doing it? Please, I don't believe for a second they will be together forever. We don't live in a fairy tale. This is real life and people break up for over the smallest thing. I'm not a pessimist but a realist. <br /><br />I need to prepare my shield because Armentrout' fangirls are going to come for me. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/520776890?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer520776890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14983940821719229181"><b>QUESTION:</b><br/><p>
  <i>What's better than a six pack?</i>
</p><br/><p>
  <b>An eight pack!</b>
</p><br/><br/><b>Kyler</b><br/><i>In reality, even though I’d been with everyone else, I’d always been Syd’s.</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795413._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Syd</b><br/><i>“I’ve loved you since you pushed me down on the playground. I swear— I’ve loved you since then.”</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795414._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First of all , I can’t believe that I'm rating a J.L. Armetrout book with 4 stars.<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380369507ra/722282.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It wasnt bad <b>BUT</b> Sydney was frustrating most of the times.<br/><br/>Secondly, shirtless guys should be <b>banned.</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795415._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401983ra/780819.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ohh WTH am I talking about?<br/><br/><b>
  <u>The story:</u>
</b><br/>Kyler and Syd grew up together. The</span>
  <span id="freeText14983940821719229181" style="display:none"><b>QUESTION:</b><br><p>
  <i>What's better than a six pack?</i>
</p><br><p>
  <b>An eight pack!</b>
</p><br><br><b>Kyler</b><br><i>In reality, even though I’d been with everyone else, I’d always been Syd’s.</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795413._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Syd</b><br><i>“I’ve loved you since you pushed me down on the playground. I swear— I’ve loved you since then.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795414._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First of all , I can’t believe that I'm rating a J.L. Armetrout book with 4 stars.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380369507ra/722282.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It wasnt bad <b>BUT</b> Sydney was frustrating most of the times.<br><br>Secondly, shirtless guys should be <b>banned.</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795415._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401983ra/780819.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ohh WTH am I talking about?<br><br><b>
  <u>The story:</u>
</b><br>Kyler and Syd grew up together. They had known each other since they were kids and they were best friends. Now that they have both grown up things and feelings have changed. They are afraid to face or admit the truth but these two liked each other for a long time.<br><br>Kyler is your typical player type and definitely off limits to Syd .On the other hand Syd hates messing around with guys because that's not her character. An annual trip to his mum's house will bring them closer.<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407308ra/795416.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Since their friends won’t make it there due to the storm, they have to stay alone. Syd's mind is going cray-cray and she starts showing her feelings. Things are awkward, actually <b>too</b> awkward but Kyler deals with them as he should and that's why I liked him.<br><br>The story is not limited only to the showing your feelings part. This couple is being sabotaged by someone. In the beginning nothing seems serious as it was expected to lose power but then it was obvious that someone was messing up with them.<br><br><b>
  <u>Kyler</u>
</b>: I liked him a lot. He was the definition of a manwhore but like all men he hadn't found someone who will care about. As soon as he realized that Syd was in love with him he started understanding his own feelings towards her too. Syd has a weird way of showing that she loves him but he doesn't want to treat her like some kind of a cheap date and that's one of his qualifications .Kyler always respected the females and Syd is not different. I loved the fact that he tried hard to gain her but the truth is that he never lost her.<br><br><b>
  <u>Syd</u>
</b>:She is the reason I'm rating this book with 4 stars. Ok I liked her but there were some moments that she needed some serious slapping.<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/474076.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I definitely get it when she is mad at him because he is fucking around. What I don’t understand is the fact that she was doubting him.<br><b>"What had he meant by that? Was he not planning to break the habit because he was still planning on sleeping around?"</b><br>Seriously??<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368016ra/720529.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I thought that she was sometimes acting like a child which bothered me a lot but thank God Kyler was there to save these annoying moments.<br><br><b>
  <u>Overall</u>
</b>: I enjoyed it a lot . It was a funny and an enjoyable book . Truth to be told it's not one of her best books but it wasn't disappointing either . I really liked the fact that Kyler wasn't the human version of Daemon Black , like Cam , but even if he was I would have still enjoyed it a lot.<br><br><b>This is forever.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407308i/795417.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews check our blog :)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/">http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14983940821719229181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458701154" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17431008384652218805">Okay, I CANNOT wait for this book. I wanna read it so bad. Plus, it's by JLA. That means there's a 100% chance I'm gonna love it to death.<br/><br/>And, aha, Kyler. Kyler Kyler Kyler. Have we all seen the drool-worthy boy for him?<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396267i/763690.jpg' width='200' height='300' alt=';)' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(His real name is Adam, by the way.)<br/><br/>Yeah. I can't even.<br/><br/>Ahhh, this cover's going to be great, and then the book is going to be even greater, and this is just going to be AWESOME.<br/><br/>Personally, I think SHP should release it, like, now. But hey, that's just me.<br/><br/>Either way, AHHHHHHHHH. <</span>
  <span id="freeText17431008384652218805" style="display:none">Okay, I CANNOT wait for this book. I wanna read it so bad. Plus, it's by JLA. That means there's a 100% chance I'm gonna love it to death.<br><br>And, aha, Kyler. Kyler Kyler Kyler. Have we all seen the drool-worthy boy for him?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396267i/763690.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt=";)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(His real name is Adam, by the way.)<br><br>Yeah. I can't even.<br><br>Ahhh, this cover's going to be great, and then the book is going to be even greater, and this is just going to be AWESOME.<br><br>Personally, I think SHP should release it, like, now. But hey, that's just me.<br><br>Either way, AHHHHHHHHH. &lt;3<br><br>OH, and it's NA. As if it couldn't get any better.<br><br>*DIES*<br><br><b>UPDATE: 1/28/2013</b><br>A teaser!! Oh. My. Gosh.<br><br><i>Strong arms wrapped around my waist from behind. I was pulled off the stool and my surprised shriek was cut off when my back hit an immoveable wall of muscle. I was enveloped in a bear hug that smelled of the outdoors and light cologne.<br> <br>Only one person in this world gave me hugs like this or felt that hard… that good. Kyler’s deep voice rumbled through my body. “When did you get here?”<br><br>My feet still weren’t touching the floor. “A little bit ago,” I gasped out, gripping his forearms through his sweater.<br><br>“What the hell? Have you been hiding from me?”<br><br>Paul leaned back against the bar and grinned, but it was strained. Not that I could blame him. Kyler kind of always busted in and took over every situation. “I haven’t been hiding,” I told him, flushing when my eyes met Paul’s. “And can you put me down?”<br><br>“What if I don’t?” he teased. “You’re so little I could put you in my pocket.” “What?” I laughed. “Put me down, you idiot. I was having a conversation.”<br><br>“Sorry, Paul, I’m stealing her.” Kyler backed away, giving me no choice, because there was no way I was breaking his hold. He turned, dropping into a chair nowhere near the table he’d been at, pulling me into his lap so I was sitting sideways. He looped his arms around my waist. “I’m not happy with you, Syd.”<br><br>I arched a brow as my heart rate picked up. He was the only person who called me Syd; the only person I let call me that without kicking them in the shin. “Really? Over what?”<br><br>“You’re talking to that douche.”<br><br>“What douche?”<br><br>He leaned in, resting his forehead against mine, and my breath stalled in my chest. Why must he always get so damn close? And he really, truly, always did. “Paul.” <br><br>“What about him?” I put my hands on his shoulders to push back, but his arms tightened, holding me in place. “Are you drunk?”<br><br>“Am I drunk? Aw, now you’ve gone and hurt my feelings, Syd.”<br><br>I smirked. “You don’t have any feelings.”<br><br>“Now. Now. That wasn’t very nice.” His impossibly long lashes lowered, shielding his eyes as he lifted his head, rubbing his cheek along mine. My fingers dug into his shoulders as desire twisted tight in my center. “I have all these feels, Syd.”<br><br>It took me a moment to respond. “You’re so full of it.”<br><br>He rubbed his cheek against me like a cat seeking a belly rub, and I fought the urge to purr. “I’m full of something.”<br><br>“Piss and vinegar?” I suggested as I desperately tried to ignore the way my pulse pounded in all the right places.”<br><br>He chuckled deep in his throat as he leaned back against the seat he took hostage. “Back to the serious nature of our conversation.”<br><br>“Which is: why are you playing Santa right now?”<br><br>Kyler’s lashes lifted and his eyes drilled into mine. “Hmm, now that sounds interesting. Have you’ve been naughty or nice this year, Syd?”<br> <br>I opened my mouth, but nothing came out. My cheeks burned as his gaze turned knowing. “I know what you’ve been.” He kissed my forehead. “You’ve been nice.”<br> <br>My shoulders slumped. I didn’t want to be nice. I wanted to be naughty like Blondie. When she’d been in his lap minutes before, I doubted Kyler had been teasing her.<br> <br>Maybe I should scoop some ice up and see what he did, except that would require me doing so out of a random glass and that was just gross.</i><br><br>Um. Did you just read that. DID YOU? It. Is. So. Amazing. <br><br>"I have all these feels, Syd." HA. That got me.<br><br>Okay, I'm going back to being dead now.<br><br>*dies*<br><br><b>UPDATE: 3/26/2013</b><br>We have a cover. An incredibly smexy cover, to be exact. I revealed it on my blog here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://justabooklover.blogspot.com/2013/03/cover-reveal-frigid-by-j-lynn.html">http://justabooklover.blogspot.com/20...</a><br><br>IT IS STUNNING!<br><br>Now back to waiting.<br><br>*dies yet again*<br><br><b>UPDATE: 6/17/2013</b><br>Look at me dying and then coming back to life not once, but TWICE. I can't help it, though. More awesomeness has been revealed. The first three chapters, an AWESOME slideshow (and by AWESOME, I mean INCREDIBLY HOT AND ATTRACTIVE), and a possibility of getting the ebook 2 WEEKS EARLY! Ahhhh!<br><br>Check it all out here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://justabooklover.blogspot.com/2013/06/frigid-preorder-promo-chapter-reveal.html">http://justabooklover.blogspot.com/20...</a><br><br>Am I the only one that noticed that "feels" has now been changed to "feelings"? I mean, it's okay, this book still looks drop dead smexy, but just saying. But that's life.<br><br>Okay, back to the dead I go.<br><br>*dies for the third time*<br><br>~~~<br><br>I'm not actually dead. And I've READ THIS AWESOME PANTS BOOK! EEEEP! It was so great. Just...AHH! There will be a review later this month!! &lt;3</span>

</a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/gif-baby-lawd-gif-1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431278ra/865317.gif" alt=" photo gif-baby-lawd-gif-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let us all bow our heads and have a moment of silence for the books you’re planning to read <b>after</b> this one.<br><br>And let us pray that they’re even <b>half</b> as good. ;)<br><br>Jennifer Armentrout AKA the <b>Yoda of sexual tension</b> does it again with this book of scrumptious amazingness! <br><br>Seriously, I didn’t even know you <i>could</i> write a sex scene like that! GEEZ! And it’s not just the way this woman can write a sex scene that makes her writing so <i>electric</i>… it’s the way she architects her characters. Sydney, for example, is so damn relatable and Kyler is so damn… SEXY! And it’s the chemistry she creates between these two that’s going to have you at the complete <b>mercy</b> of this book.<br><br>You’ll see. ;)<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/622ba39194c9b262212ae23a56b06cc0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431278i/865318.jpg" alt=" photo 622ba39194c9b262212ae23a56b06cc0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>I was Kyler’s best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him.</i>
</b><br><br>Ever since he pushed her off the merry-go-round as kids, Sydney and Kyler have been inseparable. These two were best friends and were comfortable as worn denim around each other. But people didn’t understand it. Because Sydney was the timid bookworm, and Kyler…<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/ae057b5664ca69ef4468113defa13a9c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431278i/865319._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ae057b5664ca69ef4468113defa13a9c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>\<br><br><b>
  <i>Kyler oozed sex appeal, a dangerous mix of looks and intelligence wrapped in an air of unpredictability.</i>
</b><br><br>Even as kids, Sydney loved him. And it was the innocent kind of love. The kind of love a little girl has for a little boy as they eat cold watermelon together on warm sidewalks.<br><br>But as they got older, that loved changed. <br>Because Sydney fell into it. <br><br>And as Kyler turned into that sexy, dangerous guy that turned heads everywhere he went; Sydney grew quieter and quieter how she felt about him. On the outside, you wouldn’t be able to see it.<br><br>♦You wouldn’t have seen the shards of unshed tears that glittered her eyelashes at their highschool prom when Kyler left early with another girl, and didn’t keep his promise of saving her a dance that night.<br><br>You wouldn’t have seen the way her throat held her breath captive every time Kyler gave her those bear hugs he only gave to <b>her.</b>♦<br><br>♦You wouldn’t have been able to see the way she looked at him when they had those sunrise conversations that only two best friends can have.<br><br>But now it’s their last year of college.<br><br>And Sydney has come to peace with the fact that she’ll take whatever piece of Kyler she can get. But even after so many years… she still can’t help but wonder why he’s so seemingly adamant about seducing every girl he comes across. <b>And never her.</b><br><br> Because she never <b>realized</b> that there <b>was</b> a reason why Kyler went out of his way to make sure that they would always just remain friends. <br><br><b>
  <i>Syd would always deserve far better than me, no matter how deep she lived inside of me.</i>
</b><br><br>♦Until they go on their annual winter break ski trip.♦<br><br>Because now, they’re completely alone after a blizzard completely overtakes the ski trip, causing their friends to not be able to make it; causing Sydney and Kyler to live in <i>very</i> close quarters with the other; and causing Sydney to make a friendship-shattering proposal.<br><br> <b>
  <i>“And what is it again that you want?”<br><br>I started to look away, but his fingers landed on my chin, holding my gaze to his. “I… I want you.”<br><br>“You’ve said that already. You’ve also said that you want what the other girls have gotten. You know what that is?”<br><br>I nodded the best I could.<br><br>“I fucked those girls. That’s it. No strings. No commitments. Nothing. And that’s what you want? You want me to fuck you?”<br><br>No. I wanted so much more. “Yes.”<br><br>He sucked in a sharp breath. Anger flashed across his striking face—real anger, brightening his cheeks.<br><br>“Turn around.” He ordered.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/fa6a0a3091dfae2dc8a84db5f1080d38.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431278i/865320.jpg" alt=" photo fa6a0a3091dfae2dc8a84db5f1080d38.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♦She’s always wanted him.<br>And he’s always secretly wanted her.♦<br><br>But Kyler drew lines between them for a reason.<br>Lines that Sydney wouldn’t be able to <i>uncross</i>.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/898eabf8067222d2628f835cbd404697.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431278i/865321._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 898eabf8067222d2628f835cbd404697.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>***<i>Dear Authors,<br><br>The bar has been raised.<br><br><b>And good luck.</b></i>***</span>
  <a data-text-id="7394310962703243704" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_668333992" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668333992" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/668333992?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668333992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16148561444168834479"><b>4.5 THIS IS FOREVER STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>"I was Kyler's best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429282i/859773._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Misunderstanding's, unrequited love, secrets, drama, friendships and a whole lot of snow ... 'Frigid' is a sweet, easy to read Romance and its a perfect addition to my 'easy to fall in love with' books.<br/><br/><b>What's it all about ...</b><br/>Kyler Quinn and Sydney Bell have been best friends since well, forever. They have shared life, friends and momentous occasions together but the one thing th</span>
  <span id="freeText16148561444168834479" style="display:none"><b>4.5 THIS IS FOREVER STARS.</b><br><br><b>"I was Kyler's best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429282i/859773._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Misunderstanding's, unrequited love, secrets, drama, friendships and a whole lot of snow ... 'Frigid' is a sweet, easy to read Romance and its a perfect addition to my 'easy to fall in love with' books.<br><br><b>What's it all about ...</b><br>Kyler Quinn and Sydney Bell have been best friends since well, forever. They have shared life, friends and momentous occasions together but the one thing they haven't shared is their secret love for one another, but all that changes when these two 'meant to be' characters are caught up in a snow storm which forces them to spend some quality alone time away from the distractions of Kylers man whore ways and Sydney's shy crush. <br><br><br><b>Meet the characters ...</b><br>Kyler Quinn is a loveable and equally likeable man who believes he's not good enough for the best friend he loves. The antidote to his secret feelings is to be the university's resident man whore, but with a golden heart and a face to match its not long before we see the real side of this hero. Readers be prepared to fall for Kyler, six pack, dimples and a personality to match, you'll be adding to your book boyfriend lists.<br><br>Sydney Bell has crushed so long for her best friend it's a little painful. The author created a character that is shy, a little awkward and lacking in confidence, it may be the case that some readers may find her on the annoying side, but I warmed to her wall flower ways and championed her goal to be brave and go for her man. As the story develops so does Sydney and I liked that the author choose to throw in some true to life insecurities into Sydney's inner- dialogue.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429282i/859774._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What I loved ...</b><br>The beginning of 'Frigid' definitely grabbed my attention, I was interested in how the story would play out and I was hooked with the characters from the start. I make it no secret that I love a friends who love each other/unrequited love themed story, in fact it's my favourite of all types of romance and the connection between Kyler and Sydney was heart melting. 'Frigid' certainly didn't live up to its title the connection and tension had me sitting up and taking notice, J Lynn knows how to write HOT, it might be a snow themed story but that was the only cold thing about it. This sweet story ticked all my 'loved up' boxes and I hand on heart enjoyed this book thoroughly, overall it left me with a respectable four plus star feeling.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429282i/859775._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>This story left me with a huge smile on my face, and although I rated it 4 stars there were more than a few glimpses of a 5 star story. Fans of this author or readers who enjoy a friends to lovers entertaining story should definitely try this out. A quick, sweet and at time blush-worthy romance, enjoy readers ... Go get your Kyler fix.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16148561444168834479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_668801018" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668801018" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/668801018?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=self-contained">self-contained</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=ebooks-i-own-amazon">ebooks-i-own-amazon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668801018" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10165532769655729638"><u>What a wonderful, unexpected breath of fresh air!</u> I've had such a hard time with the New Adult genre lately. Too much <b>DRAMA</b>, too much <b>ANGST</b>, too many <b>OVERREACTIONS</b> and too many <b>UNREALISTIC</b> situations. If I wanted to hear about that kind of thing, I'd go ask my ten year old about the gossip going on in her fifth grade classroom. There would be many, many BFFs crushing on the same cute boy and loads of OMG moments followed by mean girls ROTFL.<br/><br/>Fortunately, that was not the case here. Sydney and Kyl</span>
  <span id="freeText10165532769655729638" style="display:none"><u>What a wonderful, unexpected breath of fresh air!</u> I've had such a hard time with the New Adult genre lately. Too much <b>DRAMA</b>, too much <b>ANGST</b>, too many <b>OVERREACTIONS</b> and too many <b>UNREALISTIC</b> situations. If I wanted to hear about that kind of thing, I'd go ask my ten year old about the gossip going on in her fifth grade classroom. There would be many, many BFFs crushing on the same cute boy and loads of OMG moments followed by mean girls ROTFL.<br><br>Fortunately, that was not the case here. Sydney and Kyler's story felt realistic and heartwarming, just angsty enough to make my tummy clench, and ri-dic-u-lously hot sexy times without any form of BDSM theme to be found. This was truly a New Adult novel to sink into, and I did. I read it in one sitting, staying up late long after my eyes wanted to close. <br><br>Sydney and Kyler have been friends since they were six years old, back when friendship was built on simple affection. Kyler was the poor new kid in town, Sydney the sweet little girl in class. The years have gone by and they remained extremely close. Each of them secretly feels affection for the other, and not just the love of a friend. But Kyler's womanizing ways have led Sydney to feel inferior and not up to his standards. A girl's mind is an odd place to be, isn't it? Because Ryan feels exactly the opposite as she thinks he does. He's never felt good enough for her.<br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><blockquote>
  <b>" I still was the same white trash boy from the trailer park who couldn't believe he pretty little girl in class wanted to be friends."</b>
</blockquote><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><blockquote>
  <b>" Sydney was perfect - the actual embodiment of the perfect woman. She was practically pristine and fresh. She was untouchable. She was everything to me."</b>
</blockquote><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>Both are now in college, nearly graduating, in fact. Both are looking at their future not as 'the future' but as 'right now'. This is a true New Adult in the fact that Sydney and Kyler are growing up. Yes, they still like to party a bit, they still retain some freshness that is exclusive to youth. But they are also mature, looking to make decisions that will affect them for the rest of their lives. Kyler's done with the random women who have never been all that great anyways. And Sydney is tired of being the girl in the background of Kyler's life. She's ready to move on from him, ready to find her own kind of happy and stop pining over a man that will only ever be her friend.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429348i/859986.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When their group of friends heads to Kyler's family winter home on the ski slopes, they don't plan to be stuck in a wild blizzard for the entire week. But the friends get stuck on the road and have to turn back, forcing the reluctant lovebirds to spend a tension filled week alone together, with their feelings finally brought to the surface.<br><br>I felt so bad for Sydney, because she tries to be brave and let Kyler know how she feels. But everything comes out wrong, and Kyler completely misunderstands what she wants from him. He just can't fathom that she loves him like he loves her, because he's set her so far above every other girl. Not to mention that he's seen how it disappoints her to see the girls go in and out of his revolving bedroom door. He is his own worst enemy...<br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><blockquote>
  <b>" Man, I'd fucked up this morning. One fuck up among hundreds, if not thousands, and each time I was scared shitless that it would be the last time. That she would get fed up with me - with the girls, the partying , the whatever - discover that she was a thousand times better off without me, and walk out of my life.."</b>
</blockquote><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>For those of you sick of the man whore, I have to say that I actually completely forgave Kyler for his ways. He was so repentant and so down on himself. His character kind of reminded me of the promiscuous girl that we all knew in high school, sleeping around and looking for love...not realizing that they were hooching their way into loneliness. I felt bad for him.<br><br>Their feelings inevitably come to light, and sweetness and hotness ensues. I simply loved how their relationship progressed after the big revelation. The author adds a little bit of humor, more sensuality than sexuality, but still with an unexpectedly high level of steam. I was so impressed with this book, and although I'd held off on reading this author because of her obnoxious bent toward awful cliffhangers and unfinished stories, this was a fully told romance with a very definite end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10165532769655729638" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_519029381" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/519029381" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/519029381?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer519029381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4430612612836644682"><b>4.5 Stars!!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/1915cef0-6eaf-4fde-b451-bdfacc8ad0e6_zps07b5f90d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794725.jpg' alt=' photo 1915cef0-6eaf-4fde-b451-bdfacc8ad0e6_zps07b5f90d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Being in love with your best friend is rough, especially when the feelings are one sided. <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/e9aa64b1-9924-44bb-a2a9-0756899d8166_zps469d4a2e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794726.jpg' alt=' photo e9aa64b1-9924-44bb-a2a9-0756899d8166_zps469d4a2e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>I was Kyler’s best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him.</b><br/><br/>Sydney has loved Kyler for as long as she can remember. They have been best friends since they were children. Kyler is a bit of a player (understatement ;) and Syd knows he doesn’t see her that way. She won’t risk their friendship by letting him know how she feels. Even though it hurts seeing him </span>
  <span id="freeText4430612612836644682" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/1915cef0-6eaf-4fde-b451-bdfacc8ad0e6_zps07b5f90d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794725.jpg" alt=" photo 1915cef0-6eaf-4fde-b451-bdfacc8ad0e6_zps07b5f90d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Being in love with your best friend is rough, especially when the feelings are one sided. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/e9aa64b1-9924-44bb-a2a9-0756899d8166_zps469d4a2e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794726.jpg" alt=" photo e9aa64b1-9924-44bb-a2a9-0756899d8166_zps469d4a2e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>I was Kyler’s best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him.</b><br><br>Sydney has loved Kyler for as long as she can remember. They have been best friends since they were children. Kyler is a bit of a player (understatement ;) and Syd knows he doesn’t see her that way. She won’t risk their friendship by letting him know how she feels. Even though it hurts seeing him with girl after girl.<br><br>Kyler remembers when he and Sydney first became friends. He was just the boy from the trailer park, and Sydney saw past that, saw the real him. He has always cared for her. Syd is different than any other girl. She is special. She is too good for any guy, especially him. Any feelings he has for her, he covers up by being with random girls. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Syd would always deserve far better than that, and far better than me, no matter how deep she lived inside of me.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>It’s their senior year of college, and it’s winter break. Syd and Kyler are going to the ski resort like always. A huge snow storm hits. They get stranded there. Alone. While stuck alone, Kyler and Sydney are forced to deal with these feelings they have for each other. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/843af31e-81f5-4d53-afeb-dd43011ad84f_zps37e5e415.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794727.jpg" alt=" photo 843af31e-81f5-4d53-afeb-dd43011ad84f_zps37e5e415.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Kyler was AMAZING- oh so sexy, swoony and just yummy. I like Syd’s description of him... <br><i>
  <blockquote>Any female with ovaries would be affected. Kyler oozed sex appeal, a dangerous mix of looks and intelligence wrapped in an air of unpredictability.</blockquote>
</i><br>Kyler had some of the best quotes. He was charming, and endearing. I loved reading from his pov. I felt for Sydney. Unrequited love is the worst. She was sweet and funny at times. And OMG the heat between these two- WOW.<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/43cec46a-e529-48a5-b49d-63ca9c621df2_zps87d5d987.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794728.jpg" alt=" photo 43cec46a-e529-48a5-b49d-63ca9c621df2_zps87d5d987.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> Can I say ‘The Education’ scene. Those of you who have read this know exactly what I’m talking about, and if you haven’t it’s something to look forward to. <br><br><br>Really, is there anything better than a best friends to lovers story?<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/90cb46ea-13d7-4244-b949-daeebcfe8c86_zpsf2d2f184.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794729.jpg" alt=" photo 90cb46ea-13d7-4244-b949-daeebcfe8c86_zpsf2d2f184.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> I just love it. And it’s written by the fabulous J.Lynn/Jennifer Arementrout who couldn’t write a bad book if she tried. This wasn’t my favorite book of hers, but I really enjoyed it. Sweet, sexy, steamy, a small amount of suspense, and a little angsty. There is some definite miscommunication going on, which was frustrating at times. The ending was wonderful. I give it 4.5 stars! A must read for NA lovers and JLA fans! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/99e40395-6364-4a53-b0fd-02e6ff5d96ff_zpsd9b9fdbf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407052i/794730.jpg" alt=" photo 99e40395-6364-4a53-b0fd-02e6ff5d96ff_zpsd9b9fdbf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

  <span id="freeText6751185662365857082" style="display:none"> <b>5 Snow Bunnies Stars!!</b>	<br><br>Okay, I know I’m biased because I pretty much love everything that Jennifer Armentrout writes. But I’ve got to say that I loved this. Every second of it. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408225ra/798467.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, Kyler and Sydney are best friends since they were kids. <br>Sydney is a little uptight good girl that’s in love with Kyler since forever. But she knows Kyler doesn’t do the commitment thing: He sees, he does, and he leaves. And she knows that he will never see more in her that a best friend. <br>So for years she suffers, watching him with a different girl every night and knowing that she will never one of them, let along be the one who stays there all the nights. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415195i/819520.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kyler had a rough past and that made him not having the best idea about himself. <br>He’s in love with Sydney for years but he doesn’t even know why she wants to be friends with him, so why she would want to be more? <br>He doesn’t believe he deserves her so he searches for something to feel that void in other girls. Too bad that void is never filled. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415195i/819521.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But when they are stuck alone and together in the middle of a snowstorm, the pressure begins to rise and the stakes are getting higher. <br>And when things start to get unraveled, their relationship will reach a point that they’ll never be able to go back from. (I know, I’m repeating myself!) <br>I love their relationship and how it developed. Although annoying me a little, I also liked Sydney a lot. But meh, the female protagonists normally annoy me, so that’s okay. <br>I definitely loved Kyler. He is sweet, and cocky and extremely sexy. <br>Well, there’s really nothing more to say except that this is a book you can’t and will not want to miss. <br><br>Awesome buddy read with my dearest friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572523166" rel="nofollow noopener">Ana Rita.</a></span>

<div id="review_668394047" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668394047" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668394047" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1850662607432197370">3.5 ★'s<br/><br/>Kyler and Sydney have been friends forever but for quite a while, they have each wanted the other as more. Different reasons have stopped them from following through on anything. Finally, things start to change when they are stranded in a cabin during a snow storm. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/617856.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For the most part, I enjoyed this story. It's not complicated and it's an easy read. Besides the emotional yo-yo, there is some suspense but even that is easy to figure out. <br/><br/>I did like both Kyler and Sydney. They are sweet and </span>
  <span id="freeText1850662607432197370" style="display:none">3.5 ★'s<br><br>Kyler and Sydney have been friends forever but for quite a while, they have each wanted the other as more. Different reasons have stopped them from following through on anything. Finally, things start to change when they are stranded in a cabin during a snow storm. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/617856.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For the most part, I enjoyed this story. It's not complicated and it's an easy read. Besides the emotional yo-yo, there is some suspense but even that is easy to figure out. <br><br>I did like both Kyler and Sydney. They are sweet and easy to like...even Kyler with his "playa" ways especially when you find out more information about that. I loved how they knew each other for sooo long and had so many great memories. "This is Forever."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379796366i/617855.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sydney is really great but she did get on my nerves with the constantly going back and forth as far as telling Kyler. It just seemed to go on for too long! And then even after things started going, she still worried about everything. <br><br>Kyler wasn't much better and then top his problems off with his just not thinking! He did and said some things without thinking about the consequences or how it would come across. <br><br>I did enjoy Kyler and Sydney when they got together. I loved that Kyler took care of her and made things good for her. I liked that Kyler did things "differently" with Sydney...she just didn't really appreciate what that meant. It really helped getting both their POV's...I just love when authors do that! The tattoo and the picture frames were really romantic. <br><br>Andrea and Tanner are really great best friends. I was impressed how they were always there for Kyler and Sydney and I loved all their meddling. It would be interesting to see how things go between them. I saw that there is a Frigid #2 and I was hoping it would be their story but it says it's a companion. I'm guessing more of Kyler's POV? <br><br>The suspense plot added a little spice to the story...in a really creepy way. It wasn't hard to figure out who it was but I did enjoyed how it all came together. <br><br>The big question is did Kyler redeemed himself? I think he did and I liked his reasoning's. I thought it was wonderful how both Kyler and Sydney's parents acted. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/618216.gif" width="400" height="030" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Favorite quotes: (<i>slight</i> spoilers)<br><br>♥ “I want what the other girls have had.”<br><br>♥ “I will never regret being with you, Syd. <i>Never</i>. And I wish I could go back and relive those hours. I wish I could go back in time, and instead of hooking up with some chick, I’d man up and tell you how I really felt for you, how I’ve <i>always</i> felt for you.”<br><br>♥ "I've loved you my entire life," he said, eyes locked on mine. "And I would love you for the rest of my life if you'd let me, Syd."</span>
  <a data-text-id="1850662607432197370" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

She hates that he is a man-whore and a player who never says 'no' to a girl that wants to jump his bones. The only excpetion? Her.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

He doesn't deserve her, so he stays away and cherishes the only thing he can - their everlasting friendship.<br><br>But when they get caught in a snow storm, they are stuck in Kyler's mum cabin. Alone.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <b>What i thought of Sydney?</b>
</u><br>She was such an <b>annoying</b>, <b>naive</b>, and <b>stupid</b> protagonist that at times i thought 'Who the f*ck did you fall in love with, Kayler?'.<br>In my opinion him not being 'good' enough for her is a big piece of bullshit because he deserves so much more than an <b>overreacting</b>, <b>overbearing</b> and not knowing anything girl. <br><br>Kayler kisses her and she's like <i>"Why did you stop?"</i><br>Kayler pushes away from her and she's like <i>"Don't you want me?"</i><br>She does something during sex or making out and she's like <i>"You didn't like it, did you?"</i><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415308ra/819815.gif" alt="hpshutup" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><u>
  <b>What i thought of Kyler?:</b>
</u><br>Kayler i naturally <b>LOVED</b> with all my heart. <br>He was a great guy! <br><b>Protective</b>, <b>sweet</b>, <b>thoughful</b>, <b>tender</b>, and freaking <b>HOT</b>! I heart you. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415308ra/819816.gif" alt="new girl jess zooey quotes 50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>The plot is wayyy old.</b> I think i read that a thousand times already.<br> Since this is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4476934.Jennifer_L__Armentrout" title="Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer L. Armentrout</a> we are talking about, i was disappointed because i thought she would write something a bit different.<br>At times i zoomed out whilst reading and even skipped a bit. <br><br><b>What i hated the most</b> was how predictable the book was. The ending when<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sydney got attacked by Zach and the other guy and she didn't even think it might be him, she didn't recognize him (only later)<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> i was like...<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415308ra/819817.gif" alt="tumblr m5p3fh3d9b1rn95k2o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>But <b>the reason i gave this book 3</b> stars was because i personally could very much relate to falling for you best friend (been there, done that, honey), and also because the book was a bit entertaining. <br><br><b>I LOVED the sweet and hot scenes between Kayler and Sydney.</b><br><br>And after <b>A LOT </b>of the misunderstandings gets sorted out they finally get their Christmas HEA.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415308ra/819818.gif" alt="tumblr m80emqz My U1rbcx62o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Overall</b>
</u>, I liked <i>Frigid</i>. A <b>cute</b>, <b>short</b> read that i recommend you read in winter for full enjoyment :)<br><br><br><i>Sincerely - The Critic</i><br><br> <b></b><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_668014131" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668014131" />
    <a title="Marla Mei" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11172432-marla-mei"><img alt="Marla Mei" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605164478p2/11172432.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/668014131?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marla Mei" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marla Mei" href="/user/show/11172432-marla-mei">Marla Mei</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=how-about-no">how-about-no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=die-mc-die">die-mc-die</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=i-hate-myself-sometimes">i-hate-myself-sometimes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=annoying-relationship">annoying-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=yawn">yawn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=bye-bye-brain-cells">bye-bye-brain-cells</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11172432-marla-mei?shelf=fucking-hell">fucking-hell</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668014131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2559608003481282772">Edit 12/20/14: After browsing and reviewing my reviews, I can't help but notice that I sound maybe a teensy weensy bit condescending in this one. Sorry, guys. If you love this book, no probs. We cool. To those who haven't read the book, please don't let this review dissuade you from reading it. There are lots of people who found this wonderful but sadly, I am not one of them. Still, I think you should give this a try and see for yourselves. That's all. Thank you. *bows*<br/><br/>--------------------------</span>
  <span id="freeText2559608003481282772" style="display:none">Edit 12/20/14: After browsing and reviewing my reviews, I can't help but notice that I sound maybe a teensy weensy bit condescending in this one. Sorry, guys. If you love this book, no probs. We cool. To those who haven't read the book, please don't let this review dissuade you from reading it. There are lots of people who found this wonderful but sadly, I am not one of them. Still, I think you should give this a try and see for yourselves. That's all. Thank you. *bows*<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------<br /><br />After finishing Frigid, I can't help but wonder how people were even able to digest it and rave about what an awesome book it is! Really, people? This book was nothing but plain <u>
  <i>boring</i>
</u> and <i>
  <u>predictable</u>
</i>, and <i>
  <u>annoying</u>
</i> and I'm already being really generous by giving this a one-star rating. If not really for the minor characters and some funny moments, I would've totally dnfed this already. <br /><br />Frigid is just yet another clichéd story between two best friends who are secretly in love with each other and all that shit. Sydney's been in love with Kyler since like forever and though he feels the same way, too, instead of pursuing her, he did exactly the opposite and screwed around with other girls because he feels that he's not "good enough" for her and she's the kind of girl who deserves someone "better." <br /><br /><i>Seriously???</i><br /><br />Well you know what, I think that is just bullshit. If my bestfriend was secretly in love with me, I think I'd pretty much notice it. I also wouldn't deprive myself the opportunity of being with him because I'm not good enough for him or because he deserves someone better. If I wasn't good enough for him, we'd never even be best friends in the first place so that reason Kyler has there is a total bullshit.<br /><br />And if the guy and I had been best friends since preschool, I don't think it would take until we're both stranded at a ski resort for us to declare our undying love for each other. And it certainly wouldn't begin with me - for goodness' sake - begging the guy to <i>do me</i> like he does the other girls and then worrying that the guy regretted doing it with you the day after. I admire that Sydney is a woman who is aware of her sexual needs. And isn't afraid to go after them. Clap. Clap. But come on, don't go whinin' the next morning whether Kyler regretted what happened between you two. The main question is, did you? Sydney, despite being 21-years old, is not even close to being a woman. She's like a child! All she ever did was whine and overthink worthless things such as "Oh, Kyler must regret what happened to us last night." Kyler this, Kyler that. Blah blah blah. <br /><br />Congratuwelldone J. Lynn for making a character who is the epitome of stupidity. I think I just found my newest most-hated main character of all time. I think she'd be sticking in the first place for a while.<br /><br />I am practically done. There's even more actually, <i>a lot more</i> that I despised about this book and if I let myself recall and write them all here, I think I'd totally destroy myself. I'd be so done than I already am now. No, thank you. I've had enough already.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2559608003481282772" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer3447302247518278069"><i>
  <b>Almost 4 stars</b>

  <i>
    <b>"And Syd-innocent, lovely Syd-didn't have a lot of experience when it came to sex."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br/>Our Hero....<br/><blockquote>
<b><i>"Girls were like flavours to him and I wasn't o</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3447302247518278069" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Almost 4 stars</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429322i/859885._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>A friends to lover's story....what's not to love??????</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429322i/859886._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have mixed feelings about this book, on the one hand I truly loved it and then on the other there were parts which, for me, just didn't work....<br><br>It's a story told from the dual perspective of our hero and heroine which is always a bonus for me...... <br><br>Our heroine.....<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"And Syd-innocent, lovely Syd-didn't have a lot of experience when it came to sex."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br>Our Hero....<br><blockquote>
<b><i>"Girls were like flavours to him and I wasn't one he wanted to taste."</i></b> </blockquote><br><br>Kyler is not only gorgeous and handsome but musically talented as well....<br><i>
  <b>"There was nothing sexier than a guy playing the guitar."</b>
</i> ~ Sydney<br>And I have to agree...completely!!!!<br><br>I loved the hero’s inner voice straight away, charming, charismatic, just lovely!<br><br>I loved a lot of things and so wanted to love the story more but if I'm completely honest this one fell slightly short of the 4 star grade for me....yikes...I know a lot of people loved it more....<br><br>I loved the effortless writing style, the theme, the characters, the dynamic between Kyler and Sydney; their relationship and friendship is really clear to the reader but the story for me was a little disappointing. I felt it was slightly contrived in places <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ it was the guy going after kyler because of an ex girlfriend that annoyed me most, it was obvious what was happening and it just made me roll my eyes, and then Sydney did something that was just plain daft, with a stalker on the loose, imo... sorry <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I needed a little more depth and complex issues...just something more. <br><br>So, the first half of the book did not pull me in, as I would have liked, but the second half saved it for me.<br><br>From 50% on it started to HOT up....it was <i>SMOKING HOT</i> and sexy as hell....Kyler and Sydney are dynamite together...WOW...the second half of the book bumped my rating up from the 3 stars I was feeling....Phew!!!! <br><br>There were times, in the second half of the book when my heart broke for them.....<i>
  <b>I love a book that pulls at my heart strings and makes them ache!!!</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429322i/859887._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["I've loved you my entire life," he said, eyes locked on mine.   <span id="freeText17190791926127008078" style="display:none">This was a really cute friends-to-lovers romance novel. There is nothing earth shattering going on, but it gives you the warm fuzzies.
