  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859993._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo KylerQuinn_zps2c21f3e2.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Here's the kicker- Kyler has feeling for Sydney but just doesn't think that he is good enough for her......<br/><br/><a href='http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/sydneybell_zps4913fa3a.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859994._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo sydneybell_zps4913fa3a.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I am a sucker for sweet, romantic, angsty, unrequited love. Throw in some hot sex, fanning yourself "Education Sex" and you have a fabulously delicious story. This story is told in both POV's, which I love!! Being able to get into both characters </span>
  <span id="freeText15444750457179887037" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/53fe7d41-3d74-4786-9ea4-d9eb003812c7_zps7b7d6f0c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859992.jpg" alt=" photo 53fe7d41-3d74-4786-9ea4-d9eb003812c7_zps7b7d6f0c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Sydney -I was in love with my best friend. I was Kyler's best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/KylerQuinn_zps2c21f3e2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859993._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo KylerQuinn_zps2c21f3e2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Here's the kicker- Kyler has feeling for Sydney but just doesn't think that he is good enough for her......<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/sydneybell_zps4913fa3a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859994._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo sydneybell_zps4913fa3a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am a sucker for sweet, romantic, angsty, unrequited love. Throw in some hot sex, fanning yourself "Education Sex" and you have a fabulously delicious story. This story is told in both POV's, which I love!! Being able to get into both characters heads is wonderful!! This is a story of discovery, of taking chances, of love found and lost and found again.<br><br>Kyler and Sydney head out for their annual ski trip with all their friends. They ride together as they will be going home for Christmas Break after their trip. They head out earlier than their friends and after they get there, the storm of the century is coming their way...<br><b>"How much snow are they calling for?" "Somewhere between a lot and holy fuck."</b> Isn't it everyone's fantasy to be snowed in with the guy you have secretly loved for all your life!!! As you can imagine, they finally admit their feelings. It's not an easy thing and there are several mess-ups along the way. But the discovery of their love is beautiful, sad at times, steamy, heartfelt and most of all heartwarming.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/a633a02a-f2d9-4987-a433-2218bf4c409c_zps53a7a802.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859995.jpg" alt=" photo a633a02a-f2d9-4987-a433-2218bf4c409c_zps53a7a802.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"Did I think it was awesome? No. It wasn't awesome. It was the fucking best thing I'd ever felt, baby."<br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Couples/tumblr_mkx9s5zn0z1s4iwiwo1_500_zps26c7fc87.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429352ra/859996.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mkx9s5zn0z1s4iwiwo1_500_zps26c7fc87.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/7d3eca8e-8bef-4a4c-87e8-7b77e4cb6774_zps823e00dc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429352i/859997.jpg" alt=" photo 7d3eca8e-8bef-4a4c-87e8-7b77e4cb6774_zps823e00dc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>BR with my Pink Snow Angels- Barb and Jxxx ♥♥<br><br><br><br></b></span>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415139i/819380.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_moq838iGvD1rin3ljo1_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bow-chicka-wow-wow%202/tumblr_mf2xrqU5bB1rltg59o1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415139ra/819381.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mf2xrqU5bB1rltg59o1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>SYDNEY<br><br><b> I am in love with my best friend </b> <br><br>KYLER<br><br><b> She was untouchable. She was everything to me </b> <br><br><br>Sydney and Kyler were best friends forever and hide their feelings towards each other. As their annual holidays, Sydney, Kyler and bunch of mates were going skiing. Due to situation, they were stranded together and the heat turns on. They discover themselves. There was frustration, where I just wanted to know their heads together, happiness, pain and most of all LOVE.<br><br><i> "So, it's just you and Sydney? <br>Yep<br>Interesting" </i> I love Kyler's mum for that!<br><br>With snow around, it was magical. This book is really brilliant book to be read during winter. It has been a scorcher here and I am dreaming of snow. <br><a href="http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bow-chicka-wow-wow%202/tumblr_mkz2lcxSER1s91a35o1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b> "Yeah, that's how it works. I just woke up one morning and was like, 'gee I want to screw Kyler"<br>"It doesn't matter that I've been in love with you -"<br>"I've loved you my entire life"<br>"I've loved you since pushed me down on the playground" </b><br><br><a href="http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bow-chicka-wow-wow%202/tumblr_mb87jaZ4tD1qec4gro1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415139ra/819383.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mb87jaZ4tD1qec4gro1_500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Their story is sweet and adorable and again a perfect read during winter! The steam factor oh boy!!<br><br><a href="http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bow-chicka-wow-wow%202/anya-mouth-open.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_745209907" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/745209907" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/745209907?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=christmas">christmas</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer745209907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18272922422035054238"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/christmasblizzard_zps06036788.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385343655ra/7129643.gif' alt=' photo christmasblizzard_zps06036788.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I chose Frigid as an early holiday read and it was a perfect choice. This book was so sweet, sexy, sassy and even a little bit suspenseful. <br/><br/>Sydney and Kyler are in their senior year of college and winter break is just starting. These two have been best friends since the early days of elementary school, inseparable. Somewhere along the line, their feelings for each other started to evolve from friendship to something more. But neither of them wanted to jeopardize their friendship by saying an</span>
  <span id="freeText18272922422035054238" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/christmasblizzard_zps06036788.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385343655ra/7129643.gif" alt=" photo christmasblizzard_zps06036788.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I chose Frigid as an early holiday read and it was a perfect choice. This book was so sweet, sexy, sassy and even a little bit suspenseful. <br><br>Sydney and Kyler are in their senior year of college and winter break is just starting. These two have been best friends since the early days of elementary school, inseparable. Somewhere along the line, their feelings for each other started to evolve from friendship to something more. But neither of them wanted to jeopardize their friendship by saying anything.<br><br>First lets talk about Sydney. She is 21 years old and has had one boyfriend. And that didn’t end well. She could never figure out why Kyler disliked the boy she had dated so much. She has some serious insecurities but of one thing she is certain, she is madly in love with her best friend, Kyler. But she knows that she can never tell him. You see, Kyler just isn’t the commitment sort of guy. He is pretty much a man-whore. Kyler and his body to die for and those cute dimples, can have any girl he wants and he seems to want them all.<br><br>Kyler knows he feels much more then just friendship for Sydney. But she is so perfect and she deserves so much more then him. He could never be good enough for her. So he sleeps with every other girl that comes along, trying to fill the void in this heart. <br><br>Sydney and Kyler and their group of friends all have plans to go up to Kyler’s family’s ski cabin at a posh ski resort. But the weather has other plans. After Sydney and Kyler arrive, the storm of the century blows in and prevents the others from arriving and keeps Sydney and Kyler trapped in the house together forcing them to finally confront their feelings for each other. The book is written in both their POV’s and its so hilarious at times to hear what is going on in their minds. And when they finally do get together, the heat should have been enough to melt all the snow in the entire ski resort!!!<br><br>Not only do these two have to deal with their insecurities, though,it seems someone is trying to deliberately sabotage them. Is someone really trying to hurt them or just to scare them? Will they be able to stay safe until the blizzard passes and they can get help? And what will become of these newly confessed feelings once they are back in the “real world?” <br><br>I truly enjoyed watching these two not only try to resolve their feelings for each other but also, with the choices they were faced with there being only one final semester of college left and their adult lives looming ahead. This was my first NON-paranormal book that I have read by Jennifer Armentrout and it most definitely won’t be my last.<br><br>Note: This book is classified as New Adult and does contain some steamy sex scenes and some explicit language so is for appropriate readers only.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="18272922422035054238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_519005722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/519005722" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/519005722?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer519005722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2794962660309344623"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407049i/794716._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b> This was a cute, fluffy "friends-to-lovers" New Adult romance and while it was very predictable, it was also just light, sexy and fun. </b><br/><br/>It had several laughs, and a lot of steam in the second half and despite the plot being very predictable, sometimes you really need that - especially after a particularly dark or intense read.<br/><br/><div>The story is about Kyler and Sydney who had been inseparable best friends since childhood ever since he pushed her down on the playground and she made him eat a mud pie. Bu</div></span>
  <span id="freeText2794962660309344623" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407049i/794716._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> This was a cute, fluffy "friends-to-lovers" New Adult romance and while it was very predictable, it was also just light, sexy and fun. </b><br><br>It had several laughs, and a lot of steam in the second half and despite the plot being very predictable, sometimes you really need that - especially after a particularly dark or intense read.<br><br><div>The story is about Kyler and Sydney who had been inseparable best friends since childhood ever since he pushed her down on the playground and she made him eat a mud pie. But for a long time now, Sydney has been hopelessly in love with him.....<br><blockquote>
<br><div><em>"No one could replace me in his life. I knew that… I was Kyler's best friend. And because of that, he would never love me the way I loved him… Girls were like flavours to him and i wasn't one he wanted to taste." </em></div>
</blockquote>
<br>... and yet Kyler has never felt good enough for her. He'd put her on a pedestal making her both desirable and yet her unattainable for him. So he's distracted himself with other girls - anyone really…</div><br><blockquote>
  <div>
    <em>"You could put my ass in brand new sneakers, designer jeans, and a new car, and I was still the same white trash boy from the trailer part who couldn't believe the pretty little girl in class wanted to be friends… </em>
    <em>Sydney Bell had always been, and would always be, a few pedestals too high for me."</em>
  </div>
</blockquote><br>But when a snow storm strands them together in a secluded ski resort, it gives them the perfect opportunity to explore those long hidden feelings.... <br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <em>"How much snow are they calling for?"</em>
  <br>
  <em>"Somewhere between a lot and holy fuck."</em>
</blockquote><br><br>... and the colder it gets outside, the hotter things get between them and as the friend line begins to blur, their true feelings about each other come out. Oh, and let not forget the crazy stalker out there determined to ruin their time.<br><br><div>From the very first few pages, I was smiling but there was certainly a lot of back-and-forth...  Holy UST!!! There was sightly more indecision though than my usual preference in a book and by the 35% mark, I was ready to just shove them at each other and not allow them to move until they'd kissed, lol.</div><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407049i/794717._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><div>The characters insecurities were frustrating at times but at the same time I kinda just went with it. It was clear that Kyler cared for her deeply despite his man-whoring and as things began to heat up romantically between them, the swoon and hotness began to pour in.</div><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <em>"You're better than a one-night stand, Sydney. I can't do that do you… You deserve more."</em>
</blockquote><br><div>I read it in one sitting and it just cleared my palate. It was a quick, light, sometimes frustrating but fun read with a bunch of UST, no cliffhanger and a HEA.</div><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2794962660309344623" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

</a><br/><br/><b>📚 📌 FREE on Amazon US today (11/26/2017) 📌 📚</b><br/><br/>Stand-alone book 1.<br/>FREE: <b><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.amazon.com/Frigid-Book-1-J-Lynn-ebook/dp/B0741DF963/ref=sr_1_15?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1511720508&sr=1-15&refinements=p_72%3A1248987011'>https://www.amazon.com/Frigid-Book-1-...</a></b><br/>BLURB:<br/><i>For twenty-one-year-old Sydney, being in love with Kyler isn't anything new. They'd been best friends ever since he pushed her down on the playground and she made him eat a mud pie. Somewhere over the years, she fell for him and fell hard. The big problem with that? Kyler puts the 'man' in man-whore. He's never stayed with a girl longer than a few nights, and with it being their</i></span>
  <span id="freeText9356057182957395422" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIFS%20Words/free%20neon%20Pi6%20by%20sb_zpsk5aen2r3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>📚 📌 FREE on Amazon US today (11/26/2017) 📌 📚</b><br><br>Stand-alone book 1.<br>FREE: <b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amazon.com/Frigid-Book-1-J-Lynn-ebook/dp/B0741DF963/ref=sr_1_15?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1511720508&amp;sr=1-15&amp;refinements=p_72%3A1248987011">https://www.amazon.com/Frigid-Book-1-...</a></b><br>BLURB:<br><i>For twenty-one-year-old Sydney, being in love with Kyler isn't anything new. They'd been best friends ever since he pushed her down on the playground and she made him eat a mud pie. Somewhere over the years, she fell for him and fell hard. The big problem with that? Kyler puts the 'man' in man-whore. He's never stayed with a girl longer than a few nights, and with it being their last year in college, Syd doesn't want to risk their friendship by declaring her love. <br>Kyler has always put Syd on a pedestal that was too high for him to reach. To him, she's perfect and she's everything. But the feelings he has for her, he's always hidden away or focused on any other female. After all, Kyler will always be the poor boy from the wrong side of tracks, and Syd will always be the one girl he can never have. <br>But when they're stranded together at a posh ski resort due to a massive Nor'easter, there's nothing stopping their red-hot feelings for each other from coming to the surface. Can their friendship survive the attraction? Better yet, can they survive at all? Because as the snow falls, someone is stalking them, and this ski trip may be a life-changer in more ways than one.</i><br><br><br><b>FREEBIES</b> are often good for MORE than one day. <div id="review_669195280" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/669195280" />
    <a title="Amanda (.---.--.-...-)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7508641-amanda-----------"><img alt="Amanda (.---.--.-...-)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370464391p2/7508641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/669195280?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda (.---.--.-...-)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda (.---.--.-...-)" href="/user/show/7508641-amanda-----------">Amanda (.---.--.-...-)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7508641-amanda-----------?shelf=heroine-hatred">heroine-hatred</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669195280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4575789314508873887"><br/><br/>This pains me. This book, review and rating will gut me. I’m sorry Jenny.<br/><br/><b>The Good:</b><br/>The synopsis – two attractive people snowed into together with a fire place. This could have lead to some steam and swoon worthy moments. Right?<br/><br/>The dual POV - I liked hearing from Kyler because there is no way I could have only read from Sydney's woe is me voice.<br/><br/>Zach – I mean, obviously he is <i>that</i> good. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Zach, in a snow storm, can ski carrying an axe to cut down trees so they perfectly take out ones p</span></span>
  <span id="freeText4575789314508873887" style="display:none"><br /><br />This pains me. This book, review and rating will gut me. I’m sorry Jenny.<br /><br /><b>The Good:</b><br />The synopsis – two attractive people snowed into together with a fire place. This could have lead to some steam and swoon worthy moments. Right?<br /><br />The dual POV - I liked hearing from Kyler because there is no way I could have only read from Sydney's woe is me voice.<br /><br />Zach – I mean, obviously he is <i>that</i> good. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Zach, in a snow storm, can ski carrying an axe to cut down trees so they perfectly take out ones power, he can shoot and hit target during a blizzard, and he knows how to find and disable generators on random houses. I mean, that is pretty good, Right? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Zach, the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[evil <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Chuck Norris of Snowshoe.<br /><br /><br /><b>The Bad:</b><br />The plot – the virginal, self-loathing, insecure h, Sydney, and the hot, man-whore, Kyler, long-time best friends who both secretly were in love. &lt;--This just isn’t original what-so-ever. <br /><br />The lack of hair ties – Yes, you JLA fans, you know the amount of hair in face and need to for the h and H to push it back or tuck it behind her ear, was ever present and represented in every chapter.<br /><br /><b>The Ugly:</b><br />The clumsiness – I am surprised that Sydney has lived to her 21st birthday. I would have thought she would have stabbed her eye out with a butter knife or choked on applesauce while home alone. I mean, the amount of times she tripped, stubbed her toes, fell over, broke/almost broke something was ridiculous. I wish I would have counted. <br /><br />The pace – nothing happened f-o-r-e-v-e-r. I can only read so many miscommunications and lack of adult conversation for so long before my unfortunate eye-rolls are distracting enough that it actually slows down the pace to which I can flip pages.<br /><br />Sasha - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The lie Kyler told to Sydney was just pathetic…and then how he just didn’t remember doing it. I hate it when I lie, get caught, and can’t remember lying - such a little bitch. <br />Actually, my main bother is when he went to her house to help her “fix” her busted out windows. I mean, what a set-up. She wanted to lure him to her house - and hook, line, and sinker, Kyler took the bait. He just had sex with Sydney and left her alone, in a sabotaged house with zero way to communicate outside, to go help his ex-bed buddy fix her windows. Ummm, I’m not a rocket scientist but it seems like she’d have other friends or her <i>parents</i> to help her, since it was her hometown. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Sydney – I’m not sure where to start but I’ve mentioned the clumsiness and so I’ll mention the self-loathing and fear of everything was OOC. She was scared of tweezers people. She went on about how she couldn’t even pull out her own splinters. She is 21! This is not normal or cute. Then I kept thinking how did she manage to pluck her eyebrows. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I also don’t think that the wuss, Syd, would have been shot at and sprayed with glass and cuts and not mentioned it to Kyler. She is simply just too weak. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, this book was just frustrating. I was frustrated because I know JLA can write some good banter and steam. Where the eff was it? What is with the weak, insecure h? I don’t want to read about someone who does nothing but fall down, hurt herself, and compare herself to ONE comment her ex-boyfriend made over two years ago. Sigh. I’m still a fangirl of JLA. I won’t hold this one book against her. I just can’t promise I’ll recommend this book to my friends.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4575789314508873887" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15481348793101366762">My all time favorite type of love story as always been friends-to-romance, and Jennifer did such an amazing job with this book.<br/>Sydney and Kyler were some of the most frustrating and self-conscious characters I've ever read, I really wanted to bang their heads together. Hard. Repeatedly. But they were also some of the sweetest and most adorable couple I've read in a long time as well. Throughout their entire drama of self-doubts and in-your-face past mistakes, I sincerely fell in love with the wa</span>
  <span id="freeText15481348793101366762" style="display:none">My all time favorite type of love story as always been friends-to-romance, and Jennifer did such an amazing job with this book.<br />Sydney and Kyler were some of the most frustrating and self-conscious characters I've ever read, I really wanted to bang their heads together. Hard. Repeatedly. But they were also some of the sweetest and most adorable couple I've read in a long time as well. Throughout their entire drama of self-doubts and in-your-face past mistakes, I sincerely fell in love with the way these two hearts felt for one another and I simply couldn't get enough.<br />Warm, sweet and so dame delicious. <b>Frigid</b> melted my heart in all the right places. J.Lynn did it again! She's proven that no matter what she writes- Adult, YA or NA, she's a freaken Goddess! I can't wait to own this for my must-have collection. Loved!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hpQdpPtPiE1z7UA8Z1Im+aPoKafhQ9rOkO+XFBv1yKGvaq2TjtVxW/kuVUoeZfnW98dxj/kOwfaMljXUIcdMhg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vWsUbiWytyC/BogHTk3ZdVfeSo1DTbq1hrctVFIPF0iUlaRZUChONjXFnXE3egZaA/ESpVsAoY2azo+UaD2Tbw==')})
  }
